[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Introduce a configuration flag to disable remote resource fetching:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In TextAndCSVConfig [0m[1;39m([0m[39morg.apache.tika.parser.csv.TextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - A private boolean field `allowRemoteResources`, defaulting to false.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Public getter `[0m[1;35misAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and setter [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. This preserves existing behavior for callers who explicitly obtain and modify[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe config; by default, remote fetching will be turned off, closing the SSRF vector[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout breaking existing code that does not rely on embedded fetches.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Honor the new flag in TextAndCSVParser:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m251[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m262[0m[39m in TextAndCSVParser.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, before[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoking `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, retrieve the TextAndCSVConfig from the ParseContext:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        TextAndCSVConfig config = [0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTextAndCSVConfig.class[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconfig == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            config = new [0m[1;35mTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m defaults [0m[33mallowRemoteResources[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. After emitting the `<a [0m[33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"..."[0m[39m>[0m[33m...[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m>` elements, wrap the [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call in:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconfig.isAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Otherwise, skip fetching and optionally record a metadata warning or leave [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39membedding silent.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve hyperlink rendering and metadata handling:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Even when remote fetching is disabled, continue emitting the hyperlink anchor [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mso that clients still see the link text.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Avoid catching overly broad exceptions or altering existing error handling in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`processURL` itself.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Default-safe behavior:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With `[0m[33mallowRemoteResources[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m` by default, no remote connections will be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitiated during normal parsing or fuzzing, eliminating SSRF risk.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing downstream consumers who depend on embedded content can enable remote[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetching by placing a configured TextAndCSVConfig into the ParseContext:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        TextAndCSVConfig config = new [0m[1;35mTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mconfig.setAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mcontext.set[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTextAndCSVConfig.class, config[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Document the new configuration:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Update relevant javadocs for TextAndCSVConfig and TextAndCSVParser to describe[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe new `allowRemoteResources` flag, its default behavior, and how to enable it.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Testing and side-effects:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add or update unit tests to verify that, when `allowRemoteResources` is false [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mdefault[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, hyperlinks are rendered but no network calls occur, and no exceptions [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare thrown.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `allowRemoteResources` is true, parsing behavior remains as-is, including[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccessful fetches for valid URLs.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change only impacts CSV parsing remote fetching logic; it does not affect[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother parsers or utility functions.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Root cause: untrusted input leads to `new [0m[1;35mURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.openConnection[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation or opt-out.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The strategy introduces an explicit opt-in for potentially dangerous behavior [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than removing functionality altogether.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It preserves existing anchor rendering logic and avoids altering fuzz harness or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Default-off ensures backward compatibility and immediate mitigation of SSRF [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing and production use. [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:    public Map<String, Character> [0m[1;35mgetNameToDelimiterMap[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:    public Map<Character, String> [0m[1;35mgetDelimiterToNameMap[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:        this.nameToDelimiterMap = new HashMap<>[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnameToDelimiterMap[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:                          [0m[1;35m.forEach[0m[1;39m([0m[39me -> [0m[1;35mdelimiterToNameMap.put[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35me.getValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35me.getKey[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-core/pom.xml:[0m[1;36m101[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m130[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m:  <build>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m103[0m[39m:      <plugin>[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:        <groupId>org.apache.maven.plugins<[0m[35m/[0m[95mgroupId[0m[39m>[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m112[0m[39m:          <[0m[35m/[0m[95mdependency[0m[39m>[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m113[0m[39m:        <[0m[35m/[0m[95mdependencies[0m[39m>[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m114[0m[39m:        <executions>[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m115[0m[39m:          <execution>[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m116[0m[39m:            <id>validate<[0m[35m/[0m[95mid[0m[39m>[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m117[0m[39m:            <phase>validate<[0m[35m/[0m[95mphase[0m[39m>[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m118[0m[39m:            <configuration>[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m119[0m[39m:              <configLocation>checkstyle.xml<[0m[35m/[0m[95mconfigLocation[0m[39m>[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m120[0m[39m:              <inputEncoding>UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95minputEncoding[0m[39m>[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m121[0m[39m:              <consoleOutput>false<[0m[35m/[0m[95mconsoleOutput[0m[39m>[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m122[0m[39m:              <includeTestSourceDirectory>true<[0m[35m/[0m[95mincludeTestSourceDirectory[0m[39m>[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m123[0m[39m:              [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<testSourceDirectories>$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mproject.basedir[0m[1;39m}[0m[35m/src/test/[0m[95mjava[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestSourceDirectories[0m[39m>[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m124[0m[39m:              <violationSeverity>error<[0m[35m/[0m[95mviolationSeverity[0m[39m>[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m125[0m[39m:              <failOnViolation>true<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfailOnViolation[0m[39m>[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m126[0m[39m:            <[0m[35m/[0m[95mconfiguration[0m[39m>[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m127[0m[39m:            <goals>[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m128[0m[39m:              <goal>check<[0m[35m/[0m[95mgoal[0m[39m>[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m129[0m[39m:            <[0m[35m/[0m[95mgoals[0m[39m>[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m130[0m[39m:          <[0m[35m/[0m[95mexecution[0m[39m>[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We need a two-part patch:  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Eliminate the SSRF risk by guarding all remote‐URL fetches in the CSV parser [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehind a new, opt-in flag [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`allowRemoteResources`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `TextAndCSVConfig`.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Fix the Maven build break by overriding the unresolvable ASM [0m[1;36m9.7[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m dependency[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused by the Maven Compiler Plugin, forcing it to a known working version [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9.6[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. SSRF Fix in CSV Parser  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Enhance TextAndCSVConfig  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – In `org.apache.tika.parser.csv.TextAndCSVConfig`, add:  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • private boolean `allowRemoteResources = false`;  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • public boolean `[0m[1;35misAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`;  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • public void `[0m[1;35msetAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – This keeps the default behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mremote fetch disabled[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and allows [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsumers to explicitly enable hyperlink resolution via their `ParseContext`.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Guard processURL in TextAndCSVParser  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – In `TextAndCSVParser`, remove any ad-hoc new instantiation of [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextAndCSVConfig`, and instead use the class’s existing `defaultTextAndCSVConfig`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – In `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, at the top retrieve:  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `TextAndCSVConfig config = [0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTextAndCSVConfig.class, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefaultTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Wrap the call to `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconfig.isAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Importantly, this mirrors the pattern used in the `[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving customization of delimiters and other settings.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Preserve existing parser logic  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – All other cell-processing steps [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXHTML generation, link rendering[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – No harness or fuzzing code is touched.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Maven Build Fix for ASM Dependency  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The unresolved `org.ow2.asm:asm:jar:[0m[1;36m9.7[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` originates from the Maven Compiler [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPlugin’s own transitive dependency list. We override it in the `tika-core` POM:  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `tika-core/pom.xml`, under `<build><plugins>`, add [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor update[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m an explicit[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`maven-compiler-plugin` entry matching the version in use [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3.14[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```xml[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      <plugin>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        <groupId>org.apache.maven.plugins<[0m[35m/[0m[95mgroupId[0m[39m>[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        <artifactId>maven-compiler-plugin<[0m[35m/[0m[95martifactId[0m[39m>[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        <version>[0m[1;36m3.14[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mversion[0m[39m>[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        <dependencies>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          <!-- Force a resolvable ASM version -->[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          <dependency>[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            <groupId>org.ow2.asm<[0m[35m/[0m[95mgroupId[0m[39m>[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            <artifactId>asm<[0m[35m/[0m[95martifactId[0m[39m>[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            <version>[0m[1;36m9.6[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mversion[0m[39m>[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          <[0m[35m/[0m[95mdependency[0m[39m>[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        <[0m[35m/[0m[95mdependencies[0m[39m>[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      <[0m[35m/[0m[95mplugin[0m[39m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. This ensures the compiler plugin picks up ASM [0m[1;36m9.6[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mavailable on Maven [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCentral[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of the missing [0m[1;36m9.7[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, letting `mvn compile` succeed.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification & Side-Effects  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The SSRF guard is opt-in and defaults to “off,” so existing callers without an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdated `ParseContext` keep prior behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno remote fetches[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – By using `[0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, defaultTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, we honor any per-parse [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcustomizations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdelimiters, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already supported.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The ASM override is scoped only to the build plugin’s classpath; it does not [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffect runtime dependencies or other modules.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – No tests or harnesses are modified; existing unit and integration tests [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue unchanged, ensuring backward compatibility.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Potential side effect: users who did enable `allowRemoteResources` will now [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneed to explicitly call `[0m[1;35mconfig.setAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before parsing; this[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis documented as part of the API change.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The pattern `[0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mClass<T>, defaultInstance[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is already used in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. We replicate it exactly in `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Other parsers that invoke `processURL` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can adopt the same guard in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuture tickets, but only CSV requires an immediate fix per the report.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo further modifications to harness or test code are required. This strategy [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddresses both the security concern and the build break in a single cohesive patch.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • TextAndCSVParser.processURL → HttpURLConnection.connect → SSLSocketImpl.connect[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ java.net.Socket.connect → ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrfSocket.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The issue indicates that untrusted CSV cell content containing a hyperlink causes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe parser to perform an outbound HTTPS request based on data from the input, which[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF detectors flag.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The entry point is `TextAndCSVParser.parse` → `processCell` → `processURL`, not [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe harness itself.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The SSRF check triggers inside the standard Java networking classes, meaning the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparser code directly invokes URL connections.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Any CSV cell matching the hyperlink regex [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHYPERLINK_PATTERN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m leads to immediate [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote resource fetching.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exposed getter and setter: `[0m[1;35misAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Revert the unrelated POM modification:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the `maven-compiler-plugin` addition from `tika-core/pom.xml`. This [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch is not necessary for the SSRF fix and causes permission errors in the cache [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menvironment. Our focus is strictly on the Java source changes.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Extend TextAndCSVConfig to include an `allowRemoteResources` flag:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `TextAndCSVConfig.java`, after the existing delimiter getters/setters, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroduce:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private boolean allowRemoteResources = false;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public boolean [0m[1;35misAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return allowRemoteResources;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public void [0m[1;35msetAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean allowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         this.allowRemoteResources = allowRemoteResources;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures remote resource fetching is opt-in. By default [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`false`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutbound connections are attempted.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Guard all remote URL fetches in TextAndCSVParser:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Retrieve the config in every invocation of `processCell`:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In `TextAndCSVParser.java`, inside `private void [0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately after `[0m[1;35mxhtml.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`, add:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        TextAndCSVConfig config = [0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            TextAndCSVConfig.class, defaultTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Wrap the call to `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in a configuration check:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace the direct invocation:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        with:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconfig.isAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This leaves the `<a [0m[33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"..."[0m[39m>name<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m>` markup intact when remote [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresources are disallowed, but prevents the SSRF-inducing fetch.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preserve existing parsing logic and defaults:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter any other parsing flows or utility methods.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The default `defaultTextAndCSVConfig` instance remains unaffected, thus [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests and CSV parsing behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbesides embedded remote content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Validation & Testing:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add or update a unit test that sets [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTextAndCSVConfig.setAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in the `ParseContext`, feeds a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCSV cell containing an `=[0m[1;35mHYPERLINK[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://example.com"[0m[39m,[0m[32m"link"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, and asserts that:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No outbound HTTP connection is made [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcan be simulated with a stubbed [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURLConnection factory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • The output still contains `<a [0m[33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"http[0m[32m://example.com"[0m[39m>link<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m>`.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Conversely, set `[0m[1;35mallowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and verify that `processURL` is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked, embedding the remote content as expected.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By centralizing the flag in `TextAndCSVConfig`, we follow the existing pattern [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor configurable parser behavior.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Wrapping only the `processURL` call ensures minimal impact: cell-level hyperlink [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrendering remains, but network side-effects are controlled.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Reverting the POM change avoids workspace permission issues and keeps the patch [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscoped to application logic.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No harness, fuzzing, or test code is modified, preserving the existing fuzz [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargets and test suite.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach aligns with other Tika parsers that guard remote content with [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration flags [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., HTMLParser’s `setFetchExternalDTD`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensuring [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistency.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue is a Jazzer-detected Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in Apache[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika’s CSV parser: when a CSV cell contains a hyperlink, the parser unconditionally[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls `processURL`, which opens a socket/HTTPS connection to the extracted URL. A [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch was attempted to introduce a `allowRemoteResources` flag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefaulting to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`false`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `TextAndCSVConfig` and guard the `processURL` invocation in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TextAndCSVParser` behind this flag. An accompanying change to `tika-core/pom.xml` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoved a Maven plugin block. When applying the patch, the tooling reported a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“Permission denied” error on modifying `tika-core/pom.xml`, and thus the patch did [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot apply.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TextAndCSVParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m supplied input containing a CSV [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcell with a hyperlink to `jazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[39m`.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During parsing, the code in `TextAndCSVParser.processCell` uses a regex [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`HYPERLINK_PATTERN`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to detect URLs in cell content and then unconditionally calls[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `processURL` method opens a network connection via `Socket.connect` [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mHttpsURLConnection.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, triggering the Jazzer SSRF sanitizer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrfSocket`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The exception thrown is [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mForgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The CSV parser controls hyperlink detection and resolution entirely from [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no built-in opt-out or configuration guard around remote resource [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfetching in `TextAndCSVParser`.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability surface spans standard JDK networking classes, invoked from [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTika’s parsing logic.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `TextAndCSVConfig.java`:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Added a private boolean field `allowRemoteResources = false`.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Added getter `[0m[1;35misAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and setter [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `TextAndCSVParser.java`:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Retrieved the `TextAndCSVConfig` from `ParseContext` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalling back to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefaults[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Wrapped the call to `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconfig.isAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `tika-core/pom.xml`:  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Removed a block related to the Maven Compiler Plugin [0m[35m/[0m[39m Clirr Plugin [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcomment[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates “Removed maven-compiler-plugin block”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Application Result  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The automated patch application failed with:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     “Permission denied: [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'/home/qqor/crete/.cache/official-afc-tika/tika-core/pom.xml'[0m[39m cannot be modified [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbecause it is not a valid language file.”  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This indicates that the file system or tool configuration prevented modifying [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-core/pom.xml`, so the patch was not applied.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All parser modules that may fetch external resources [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., HTML, XML, OOXML [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should be audited for similar unguarded remote access.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The mechanism by which `TextAndCSVConfig` is instantiated and injected into [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParseContext`—ensure that consumers can set `allowRemoteResources` as intended.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The implementation of `processURL` itself: verify it does not rely on any [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother unvalidated redirects or follow-ups.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Build configuration under `tika-core/pom.xml` and repository permissions to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand why the patch could not be applied to that module.[0m                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m247[0m[39m:    private void [0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cellContent, XHTMLContentHandler xhtml,[0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m250[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mxhtml.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m258[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mxhtml.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"a"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"href"[0m[39m, url[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m259[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mxhtml.characters[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m261[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m262[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Introduce an opt-in flag in the CSV parser’s configuration to disable all [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote-resource fetching by default. By default, `[0m[33mallowRemoteResources[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m`, so [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many hyperlink detected in a CSV cell will still be rendered as an `<a [0m[33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"..."[0m[39m>` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the XHTML output but will not trigger the network call. Users who explicitly [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrust the CSV input [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in a secure internal context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can toggle the flag to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`true` via `ParseContext` or the Tika configuration framework.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. TextAndCSVConfig changes  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `TextAndCSVConfig.java`, import Tika’s configuration annotation:  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      `import org.apache.tika.config.Field;`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Declare a new private boolean field with the `@Field` annotation and default [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit to `false`:  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      @Field[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private boolean allowRemoteResources = false;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Provide a public getter and setter following JavaBean conventions:  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      public boolean [0m[1;35misAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m return allowRemoteResources; [0m[1;39m}[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      public void [0m[1;35msetAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean allowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis.allowRemoteResources = allowRemoteResources; [0m[1;39m}[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This mirrors Tika’s existing patterns, allowing the field to be bound from [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML/properties-based configuration or programmatically via `ParseContext`.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. TextAndCSVParser changes  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `TextAndCSVParser.java`, locate the `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method where [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhyperlinks are detected [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m250[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Retrieve the `TextAndCSVConfig` [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready exposed via [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mcontext.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTextAndCSVConfig.class, defaultTextAndCSVConfig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Wrap the existing unconditional call to `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` behind the new [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mflag:  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconfig.isAllowRemoteResources[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This preserves hyperlink rendering in the XHTML but prevents the network fetch [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munless explicitly enabled.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No changes to build files or fuzzing harness  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The attempted removal of the Maven plugin block in `tika-core/pom.xml` is not [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequired for this fix and may conflict with repository permissions. Omitting that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange ensures the patch applies cleanly.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not touch fuzzing or test harness code; tests will continue to exercise [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`processURL`, but by default the code path is bypassed, so no SSRF crash will [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccur.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Documentation and tests  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Update the CSV parser’s module documentation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJavadoc or `parser-config.xml`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto describe the new `parser.csv.allowRemoteResources` property [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor equivalent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits default value.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a unit test that simulates a CSV cell with a hyperlink: verify that with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[33mallowRemoteResources[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m` the network code path is not invoked [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., by mocking[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`processURL` or using a fake `ParseContext`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and that with [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[33mallowRemoteResources[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m` the call proceeds.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Audit other parsers  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After fixing CSV, schedule an audit of other Tika parsers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., HTML, XML, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOOXML[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for similar unguarded remote-resource fetch code and apply the same pattern.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhy this is optimal  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It directly addresses the SSRF issue by disabling remote fetch by default, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimizing the attack surface.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It preserves existing parsing and XHTML-rendering logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinks still appear[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It leverages Tika’s standard `@Field`-based configuration, ensuring seamless [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintegration with `ParseContext` and the broader Tika config framework.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By not touching `tika-core/pom.xml`, we avoid permission and tooling conflicts.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No fuzz harness modifications are needed, so the fix integrates smoothly with [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting tests and fuzzers.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The approach is consistent with patterns in other Tika parsers that guard [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal lookups behind config flags.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Side effects are limited: users must explicitly opt in to potentially dangerous [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior, and safe defaults are maintained.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Future audits of similar code can reuse this pattern.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
